### Papers / 2023

*   [Modeling rabbit‚Äëholes on YouTube](https://link.springer.com/epdf/10.1007/s13278-023-01105-9?sharing_token=h-O-asHI49VUWS9FxN1Gsve4RwlQNchNByi7wbcMAY6I98PKW1PqhFQJ_JqQyk3TrB05qDb3LUzMDmKOgrupccQliViDle-rwKEi2MZ8xBViaAQhyN41oZBKLLeXchoeIW2kklVHC094I5KD8pxja4-if6-iB0uAI1FnqnYoxjU%3D) - (SNAM) *Models the trapping dynamics of users in rabbit holes in YouTube, and provides a measure of this enclosure.*
*   [Auditing YouTube‚Äôs Recommendation Algorithm for Misinformation Filter Bubbles](https://dl.acm.org/doi/full/10.1145/3568392) - (Transactions on Recommender Systems) *What it takes to ‚Äúburst the bubble,‚Äù i.e., revert the bubble enclosure from recommendations.*

### Papers / 2020

*   [Auditing radicalization pathways on ](https://dl.acm.org/doi/pdf/10.1145/3351095.3372879) - (FAT\*) *Studies the reachability of radical channels from each others, using random walks on static channel recommendations.*
